<Name>Buckley Dueker<//Name><Text>Great for a small shop! Good but small selection of hand picked retail releases at prices you'd expect. The staff picks are fun to look through and are interesting and eclectic. They are often playing some really interesting tunes as you browse. The staff is friendly and helpful, but I can't help but pick up a bit of that pretentious hipster vibe on occasion.

Used releases are in good condition but priced on the high side of collector value. You won't make a profit by buying and flipping from here, but it's a good place to find that first pressing you've been looking for at a reasonable market price.

Used vinyl in the dollar bins underneath has no organization, so be prepared to dig. Here is where you might find some gems. It won't be incredibly rare or valuable, but some of my favorite tracks have been found here and they're in relatively good condition.

My only complaint is that the reggae selection is seriously lacking, but that seems to be the case for both of the main vinyl sources in downtown Santa Cruz. I'm not sure why that is... I know it's a popular genre in the area.<//Text><Pics>None<//Pics>< Resp>

<userid>111743770667590548068<//userid><text>This is my favorite record store. The staff is very knowledgeable and in no way pushy or in your face. The layout is simple yet expansive. There's an excellent selection of pristine new records, and a massive array of used records. The back wall holds the dollar bin, which in my eyes is the store's greatest asset. They get donations all the time from DJs and collectors, and don't have the time or man power to sort through and price each record. It's more cost efficient for them to just put it all on sale. Thus, you can find some truly exceptional stuff for a dollar. I've bought records of Miles Davis, John Coltrane, Freddy Hubbard, Guru, Company Flow, Talking Heads, Elvis Presley -- a wide array of true classics from every genre, some in near mint condition still in shrink wrap, for $1. You should shop here if you like music.<//text><Gmap_id>0x808e6a9d45b367d5:0xa8516b46e56a3f43</Gmap_id>< Time>

Metavinyl is nice little gem of a record shop. Like most record shops these days they are dominated by newly pressed vinyl but their used selection is pretty good considering the size of the place. I found 4 used records and paid just over $10. New vinyl is the same price you'd pay almost anywhere.
I visited on a Monday so it was easy to find metered parking.
I would prefer a bit more organization of the bargain bins. They are somewhat alphabetical but everything is so mixed up that you have to search each bin to maybe find what you're looking for.
I definitely recommend a stop at Metavinyl if you're in Santa Cruz.<//Review>

< Text>
Metavinyl has a lot of treasures in all sorts of genres.  A really great selection of used records, but not a lot of "deals" to be found.  Prices are fair and in line with what you'd pay online at Discogs, but you aren't going to find raging deals.  You will find some pretty rare stuff, though.  An absolutely worthwhile shop that carries only records and stuff you'd use to play them. (Actually, they may have a couple of dozen cassette tapes, too).

Their new selection is large for a small shop, but not extensive.  I mainly shop the used bins.</Text>

<text>Trying to donate to Habitat for Humanity is not worth the effort. I had 18 window blinds in relatively good condition to donate. I called ahead and was told they accept blinds no problem. I packed the blinds and the connectors, and accessories, and drove 1/2 hr to get there. Once I arrived an unfriendly worker at the store (Richard) took one look at the blinds and told me they can't take any because some have speckles of dry wall in some places. He told me in an arrogant tone "if I want to clean all the blinds and then bring them back", they might accept them!!! I did not realize donations should include maid service! Fortunately a very kind lady who was at the store to shop, took all the blinds and said she had  rentals and can put them to good use.  The moral of the story is think twice before donating to this outfit. < Text>
The Habitat for Humanity Restore Store is a wonderful place to browse for all sorts of items for your home. Are you a renter whp doesn't want to give up all of your LED bulbs when moving out, but don't feel like paying retail for the incandescent or CFLs that you didn't bother to save or burned out? The Restore Store has hundreds of them at ridiculously cheap prices.  Or are you a landlord dealing with a messy eviction where the tenants trashed everything before finally being forced to leave? The Restore Store had everything from toilets to light fixtures to cabinets and cabinet hardware at a fraction of what Home Depot or Lowe's charges!  Do you need some cheap but  sturdy  furniture for your first apartment? They have that, too.  Or are you a contractor or business with excess inventory or anything construction or home/office related and need a tax write-off? Donate your stuff to the Restore Store and you can be assured that the proceeds will go for a worthwhile cause that does great work both here in the U.S. and abroad. And it is fun to shop there!  One month I bought a cat tree, the next month an electric drill,  the next month some drawer handles to replace ones that had broken. Every time I go, the inventory changes with new items coming and going constantly! Check them out; you won't be sorry that you did!</Text>

<Review>Nothing but positive things to say. This dude is AWESOME.

I specifically requested a referral to Dr. Buddiga because I'd read about his research and activism regarding pollution in the Central Valley and how it impacts the people who live here. He seemed like a doctor who truly cares about his patients, so I asked to see him before anyone else. Unlike most quality doctors in this town, he accepts my low-income insurance, and I was approved much more quickly than most specialist referrals. They called me and offered an appointment within less than a week of the phone call!

Office staff is very friendly, helpful, and fast. Very efficient and up-to-date. Dr. Buddiga is kind and patient, will answer all of your questions, and respects your time. He'll listen to whatever you have to say and proceed with whatever works for you as an individual.

My first appointment was quick, I was seen immediately and within minutes I was given a food allergy test. When the results were all negative he ordered blood work, and offered me an environmental allergy test just a week later. When I got that test, I lit up like a Christmas tree. He discussed with me the option of immunotherapy shots, fully transparent about the commitment it requires, and said we'd only proceed once I was ready. In the meantime he told me which OTC allergy meds would best supplement my current treatment. He scheduled an appointment in a few months, and said to call and make one sooner if I was ready before then.

I've had a lot of horrible experiences with doctors in this town, especially suffering from chronic illnesses and low income. Dr. Buddiga is every exception. I've already recommended him to several people and will continue to do so. I look forward to working with him in the future.
